CHANGELOG v7.31 → v7.32:

  TRIGGER: External PT4-based leak report cross-reference exposed gaps
  in our pipeline's per-position decomposition. 11 enhancements (C1-C11)
  scoped end-to-end. v7.31 already shipped Parts A+B from the original
  Implementation_Prompt; v7.32 is Part C only.

  C1 PER-POSITION TURN CBET: New chart family TURN_CBET_TARGET_<POS>
     (47-57% all positions) in Poker_Ranges_Text.txt. New core stat
     core['turn_cbet_by_pos'] keyed by Hero position with opps/count/pct
     dict. Numerator: parser's `double_barreled` flag. Denominator: PFR +
     cbet flop + saw turn + not faced_xr_after_cbet (i.e., cbet got
     called, not raised). New detector_turn_cbet_by_pos compares to
     target band, emits dev records with CLEAR/MARGINAL confidence.
     Report section: Del 2D+ (table) + Del 2N+++a (deviations).

  C2 PER-POSITION RIVER CBET: Same pattern as C1 with RIVER_CBET_TARGET_*
     chart family. Numerator: parser's `triple_barreled`. Denominator:
     double_barreled + saw river + not bet_then_faced_raise_turn (proxy
     for "turn barrel got called HU").
     Report section: Del 2D++ + Del 2N+++b.

  C3 PER-POSITION FOLD-TO-FLOP-CBET: F2CB_TARGET_* family with band shape
     varied by position (BB widest 40-45%, BTN tightest 27-33%, EP middle
     33-38%). Surfaces the "external report flagged 6/6 positions over-
     folding while aggregate read in-target" pattern. Couples with C10
     aggregate-masking detector for headline warning.
     Report section: Del 2D+++ + Del 2N+++c.

  C4 4-BET TARGET BAND CORRECTION (5-8% → 12-20%): Denominator was fixed
     in v7.31.1 ("Hero opened then faced 3-bet" — only spot 4-bet is an
     actual decision) but target band lagged at the legacy 5-8% from the
     old "% of all opens" definition. v7.32 updates to 12-20% (GTO-typical
     for the corrected decision space). Adds explicit aliases:
       core['hero_4bet_when_facing_3bet_pct']
       core['hero_4bet_when_facing_3bet_n']
     Plus per-position decomposition core['hero_4bet_by_pos'].
     IMPORTANT: when reading old reports, mentally rebase the 4-bet
     line. Sessions where Hero 4-bet was 🟢 in the legacy 5-8% range are
     now 🔴 (below the correct 12% floor).
     Report section: Del 2C+.

  C5 SB LIMP FOLLOW-THROUGH: After Hero limps SB and BB raises, what
     does Hero do? New core stats sb_limp_call_pct (target 45-55%),
     sb_limp_raise_pct (10-14%), sb_limp_fold_pct (35-45%). Plus
     diagnostic stats sb_fi_n / sb_raise_first_pct / sb_limp_open_pct /
     sb_fold_first_pct. Coaching priority unchanged: Dave's J29 80/10/10
     governs the limp-vs-raise decision (Del 2L); this sub-table only
     addresses post-limp follow-through.
     Report section: Del 2L+ (renders only when sb_limp_then_raised_n >= 5).

  C6 PER-POSITION RFI DEVIATION FLAGGING: New detector_rfi_by_pos
     compares pos_data[p]['open_pct'] to RFI_TARGET_<POS> bands. SB
     intentionally targeted 70-90% per Dave's J29 (overrides external
     report's 35-42% raise-frequency target — coaching hierarchy
     Dave > Jaka per memory). Targets are depth-mixed at 100BB; report
     notes "tighten <40bb" as caveat for non-SB rows.
     Report section: Del 2N+.

  C7 SQUEEZE BY POSITION: New parser field `squeeze_opp` decouples the
     squeeze opportunity denominator from Hero's action (was previously
     conflated with hero_3bet logic). Defined as: opener seen + at least
     one cold-caller before Hero's first PF action. New core stat
     core['squeeze_pct_by_pos']. Targets band per position (BB widest
     9-15%, EP narrowest 4-7%). New detector_squeeze_by_pos emits dev
     records.
     Report sections: Del 2C++ (table) + Del 2N++ (deviations).

  C8 DETECTOR_REQUIRED_CHARTS REGISTRY (gem_quality.py):
     New module-level registry mapping each detector to chart-family
     prefixes it requires:
       check_open_deviations:        OPEN_100BB_*, OPEN_20-40BB_*, PUSH_10BB_*
       check_rejam_deviations:       REJAM_*
       check_defend_3bet_deviations: CALLRJ_*, FLAT3B_*
       check_bb_defend_deviations:   BB_DEF_*
       check_turn_cbet_by_position:    TURN_CBET_TARGET_*  [v7.32 new]
       check_river_cbet_by_position:   RIVER_CBET_TARGET_* [v7.32 new]
       check_fold_to_cbet_by_position: F2CB_TARGET_*       [v7.32 new]
       check_squeeze_by_position:      SQUEEZE_TARGET_*    [v7.32 new]
       check_rfi_by_position:          RFI_TARGET_*        [v7.32 new]
     New preflight_check_detector_charts() walks the registry; if a
     required chart family has zero matching loaded entries, detector is
     flagged unreliable in pre-flight. Catches the v7.30 silent-zero
     failure pattern (56 missing CALLRJ_*/FLAT3B_* charts → Missed-Defend
     reported 0 deviations and looked clean).

  C9 BUY-IN BOUNDS PREFLIGHT: New preflight_check_buyin_bounds() warns if
     any parsed buy-in exceeds $5,000. Tripwire for v7.31's filename-
     format-change parser bug ($20.26M reported because date misread as
     buy-in). Actual fix is in gem_report_data.py _parse_buyins; this
     check is a regression guard.

  C10 AGGREGATE-MASKING DETECTOR: When an aggregate metric is 🟢 in-target
      (n>=30 for aggregate) but ≥3 positional decompositions are out-of-
      band (CLEAR/MARGINAL each, n>=10 each, total positions evaluated
      >=5), emit AGGREGATE_MASKS_LEAK_<metric> finding stored at
      stats['aggregate_masking']. Currently runs on fold_to_cbet (band
      50-60%) and turn_cbet (band 47-57%). Reportable as Del 2N+v
      "Aggregate-Masking Warnings". Inline warning also surfaces under
      Del 2D+++ (Fold to Cbet table).

  C11 STRUCTURE_PROFILE + SKILL_BAND: hero_classification was being
      misread as a SKILL judgment ("Average") when it's a STRUCTURE
      metric (FT-zone %). v7.32 splits:
        rd['structure_profile']: alias of hero_classification
        rd['skill_band']: derived from EV BB/100 + 95% CI on bb-per-hand
      Skill band thresholds:
        Crusher:     lower CI > +10 BB/100
        Strong reg:  lower CI > +5 BB/100
        Solid reg:   lower CI > 0
        Marginal:    CI straddles 0
        Losing:      upper CI < 0
        Insufficient Sample: n_hands < 200
      Both surface in Del 0 TLDR. hero_classification kept as alias for
      one version (v7.32) — will be removed in v7.33.

  PATH RESOLUTION: gem_analyzer.py now prefers Poker_Ranges_Text.txt co-
  located with the analyzer module over /mnt/project/ snapshot, so
  in-development edits take precedence. Matches test_detectors.py pattern.

  TEST FIX: test_squares.py snap_has_version assertion bumped 7.26 →
  7.32 (was stale since v7.27, silently failing).

  TEST COVERAGE ADDED: 32 new assertions in test_metrics.py covering all
  v7.32 core stats and preflight checks. Total test count: 457 (up from
  425). All structural — full suite (1063 tests) passes minus 2 pre-
  existing baseline failures (FT Flat Alert, texture archetypes — unchanged).


CHANGELOG v7.24 → v7.25:

  PROCESS — NEW LEARNING INTAKE CHECKLIST:
    Mandatory 5-step process (Classify → Component Impact Matrix →
    Ask Before Building → Version + Changelog → Ship) added near
    top of Instructions file (before RULE CODE FORMAT STANDARD).
    Short-form pointer added to Quick Reference. Triggered by
    Ron's catch on v7.24: J43/J44 shipped as documentation when
    code was needed. New triggers: every coaching insight (Dave,
    Amit, Jaka, MoP, podcast, book, GTO solve) walks through this
    matrix BEFORE any file edits. Retroactive demonstration on
    J41-J44 included in this changelog cycle.

  J43 DETECTOR EXPANSION (was: doc-only in v7.24):
    Original FT Flat Alert detector renamed to ICM Flat Alert.
    Old trigger: opener ∈ {EP/MP} + level≥15 + n_pl<ts + stack<80.
    New trigger: tournament_phase ∈ {bubble_zone, post_bubble,
    ft_zone} + Hero position ∉ {BTN, BB} + Hero VPIP'd without
    PFR'ing + opener was ANY position + stack<80. Confidence
    remains MARGINAL with requires_confirmation=True. Subject
    to Leak Validation Gate before promotion to confirmed leak.
    Rationale: J34 detector handles MP <=30BB ICM specifically;
    J43 generalizes to all non-BTN/BB positions in any ICM
    phase. Cross-references J34 (specific case) and J43 (broad
    principle).

  J44 PARSER + ANALYZER + REPORT WIRING (was: spec-only in v7.24):
    PARSER (gem_parser.py):
      Added hero_3bet_size_x field to hand records. Computed as
      hero's preflop 3-bet to-amount in BB / opener's raise
      to-amount in BB. Captured during preflop loop when
      pf_raise_count transitions 1→2 with Hero as the raiser.
      Null when Hero didn't 3-bet (no opener or no Hero raise).
    ANALYZER (gem_analyzer.py):
      Added ip_3bet_sizing tracker. Buckets all Hero IP 3-bets
      (CO/BTN/HJ) by stack depth (<25BB, 25-40BB, 40+BB) and
      records target sizing (2.5x, 3.0x, 3.5x respectively).
      Flags hands where |actual - target| > 0.5x as deviations.
      Tracker exposed on s['ip_3bet_sizing'].
    REPORT DRAFT (gem_report_draft.py):
      Added Del 2I++ section "IP 3-Bet Sizing by Depth (J44)"
      after Sizing Consistency Score. Shows actual vs target
      per bucket, count of hands, deviation flags.
    TESTS (test_parser.py + test_detectors.py):
      New parser assertions verify hero_3bet_size_x extraction.
      New detector fixtures cover (CO, BTN, HJ) × (<25, 25-40,
      40+) × (correct/oversized/undersized) sizing scenarios.

  MANUAL ADD PROTOCOL — ICM CONTEXT STEP H:
    Existing checklist (steps A-G) gains Step H. Applied during
    Del 4B mistake review for hands in bubble_zone+ phases.
    Encodes:
      H1. ICM directionality (J41) — who's the aggressor, who's
          the responder; verify chip_leader_cover_jam tag matches
          actual hero-as-short-caller direction.
      H2. Ladder value (J42) — estimate pay jumps within reach
          at 2x BI per jump; weigh chip-EV vs ladder $ value.
      H3. Raise-or-fold lens (J43) — for any flat-call in ICM,
          ask: was 3-bet or fold the better line?

CHANGELOG v7.23 → v7.24:

  DAVE COACHING SESSION 2026-04-29 — ICM PRINCIPLES + IP 3-BET SIZING:

  Four new J-rules added to Appendix J continued. All sourced from
  Dave session covering ICM range dynamics and preflop sizing:

    J41. ICM Range Asymmetry — short stack narrows ranges (>50%
         in some scenarios), big stack as aggressor expands. Direction
         matters: when short stack JAMS, big stack RESPONDER narrows
         (this is the inverse of when big stack opens vs short).
         Codifies the asymmetric risk-premium principle that already
         underlies M8/M10/Appendix D but was never stated as a single
         explicit rule with directional caveat.

    J42. ICM Ladder Heuristic — every pay jump ≈ 2x buy-in worth.
         Quick mental model for risk premium estimation without
         ICMizer. Useful at the table when evaluating "should I take
         this spot" vs ladder protection.

    J43. ICM Raise-or-Fold (generalized) — when a hand is not
         strong enough to call in ICM, the correct line is raise
         or fold, not flat-call. Generalizes J34 (which is MP-
         specific at <=30BB) to broader ICM contexts. Cross-
         references J34 for the precise auto-detected case.

    J44. IP 3-Bet Sizing by Depth — <25BB: 2.5x. >40BB: 3.5x.
         25-40BB: linear scale (~3x mid-range). Companion to J30
         (BB 3-bet = 5x OOP). Auto-detector spec included; parser
         work to extract numeric 3-bet ratios required before
         the flag is wired into analyze_session.

  ANALYZER WORK PENDING (v7.24.1):
    - Parser: extract Hero's preflop 3-bet amount in BB and
      opener's raise amount in BB from pf_sequence (currently
      hero_bets only tracks postflop).
    - Analyzer: position-bucketed sizing tracker (CO/BTN/HJ
      separate from BB), depth bucket (<25, 25-40, 40+), flag
      |actual - target| > 0.5x as deviation.
    - Tests: add to test_detectors.py, must pass full 54+
      assertion suite.

CHANGELOG v7.22 → v7.23:

  LIVE POKER POPULATION REFERENCE (2026-04-24, APT Day 1+2 debrief):

  NEW FILE: Live_Poker_Population_Reference.txt — codifies live
  MTT pool calibration deltas vs online baseline. Sits alongside
  Mental_Game_Reference.txt as a standalone reference consulted
  during Del 4B mistake review when session FORMAT indicates live.

  CONTENT COVERED:
    - Preflop range differences: limp ranges include 77-TT/JJ
      ("bingo style", confirmed by Dave); suited Axs flats go deep
      (A7s-A9s in flat ranges, not just ATs+); wide flat ranges
      include broadway floaters but they're curious passives, not
      aggressive bluffers; 3-betting tighter than online.
    - Postflop tendencies: sticky TPGK (Ax doesn't fold to medium
      river sizing); under-bluff rivers especially overbets;
      station-y with pairs once invested; floaters don't bluff
      rivers when checked to.
    - Dave's bluff sizing tree: small flop c-bet (~20% pot) →
      big turn barrel (75-85% pot) as polarizing scare-card bet
      to deny 2-out equity from sticky pairs → give up river
      against capped ranges. Turn is the last profitable bluff
      street. Anti-pattern: medium-medium-big sizing (online-
      style) builds pot into stickiest zone.
    - Decision-tree fixes: "no SDV → shove" replacement (zero
      SDV only rules out check-calling, doesn't make bluff
      correct); c/r turn OOP from preflop flat-caller is value-
      heavy (~85-95%) at live APT, AK/TPTK calls are -EV; AK/
      TPTK on dry A-high OOP-capped 50-80BB = c-bet flop / check
      back turn / act on river by sizing.
    - Pool-specific exploits: value-bet relentlessly vs sticky
      Ax/pairs; overfold vs overbets from capped lines; don't
      hero-call rivers (MDF doesn't apply to under-bluffing pools);
      punish limps via wider iso from LP.
    - Red flags / anti-patterns: running online sizing tree at
      live without recalibration; committing to multi-street
      plans dependent on FE pool doesn't supply; chip-lead
      confidence widening hand selection; post-bullet desperation
      tilt widening ranges on re-entry.
    - Pre-session warm-up: 5-bullet checklist for live MTT entry.

  NEW DETECTOR_BUG TAXONOMY TAGS (valid values for
  gem_exceptions_log.csv detector_bug column):
    pool_calibration_online_bluff_vs_live — bluff line +EV online
        but -EV live due to pool range composition (Axs flat
        depth / sticky pairs / under-bluff floaters).
    pool_calibration_c_r_turn_oop — c/r turn OOP from preflop
        flat-caller is value-heavy at live APT; AK/TPTK calls -EV.
    pool_calibration_no_sdv_shove — "no SDV → shove" against
        capped + sticky live range; check-fold is +EV.

  Remediation for pool_calibration mistakes: re-read
  Live_Poker_Population_Reference.txt before next live session,
  not re-study bluff theory. Different remediation path than
  standard skill-leak mistakes.

  INTEGRATION:
    - Cross-reference added to file pointer block (after
      Mental_Game_Reference.txt line).
    - Quick Reference v7.23 changelog block + cross-reference
      pointer added.
    - Reviewer module in gem_flag_reviewer.py: when session
      FORMAT indicates live (LIVE_MTT tag), consult this
      reference before confirming bluff-line mistakes.
      (Auto-detector wiring deferred — manual review pattern
      matches Mental_Game_Reference.txt precedent.)

  FUTURE WORK FLAGGED (not in scope for v7.23):
    - FORMAT=LIVE_MTT parser tag wiring (parser_config update
      to recognize live session imports).
    - Auto-detector hooks for live-pool-specific patterns
      (requires 5+ more live sessions of data for stable
      signatures).
    - Promotion to Appendix N (rule codes L1, L2, etc.) once
      framework is battle-tested across multiple live sessions.


CHANGELOG v7.20 → v7.21:

  MANUAL ADD PROTOCOL (afternoon of 2026-04-21, Session 20 debrief):

  Architecture clarification: the FLAG REVIEW LAYER (v7.20) handles
  hands the analyzer flags. v7.21 adds the symmetric protocol for hands
  the analyzer correctly does NOT flag — preventing Claude from
  manually-adding losing PFR all-in hands as "punts" without first
  doing the equity math.

  Rationale: Session 20 (2026-04-21) — Claude added two hands as
  "manual confirmed punts" that the analyzer correctly didn't flag
  (AQo UTG 33.5BB call vs SB cold-jam, KQs MP 29BB 4-bet jam vs HJ
  3-bet). Both decisions were defensible vs Hero's actual reads:
    - AQo: 38.2% equity vs Hero's stated villain range (88+/AQo+/AJs/ATs+),
      need ~40% with bounty premium → slight -EV (~-2 to -4BB), not
      a -10BB punt.
    - KQs: standard fold/shove framework at sub-30BB IP. With KQs
      blockers (KK, AK, AQ) + villain known to 3-bet light + 50%+
      fold equity to 4-bet jam → EV(jam) ≈ +1.5BB vs EV(fold) ≈
      -2.2BB → jam +EV.
  Both hands re-classified as "Read-Dependent Decisions" not punts.
  Logged to exceptions_log entries 6-7 with manual_punt_overclassification
  tag.

  Required analytical checklist for ANY preflop near-all-in spot
  (codified in Quick Ref MANUAL ADD PROTOCOL section):

    A. POT ODDS — chip equity needed (amount-to-call / total-pot)
    B. VILLAIN RANGE — with context tag (standard / squeeze / cover /
       micro / read-driven / wide-population). USE the wider range if
       context widens it.
    C. BOUNTY ADJUSTMENT — covers Hero or Hero covers? Premium
       calculation reduces required equity by 3-7pp typically.
    D. EQUITY vs RANGE — actual % weighted by remaining combos
       (Hero's blockers reduce villain combos)
    E. BLOCKERS — what does Hero block from villain's value range?
       (Critical for jam-with-blockers spots like KQs blocking KK/AK/AQ)
    F. FOLD EQUITY — applicable when Hero is initiator (jammer/raiser).
       0% FE when Hero is calling all-in. FE × pickup vs FE × showdown EV.
    G. EV CALCULATION — EV(action) vs EV(alternative) in chips and BB,
       across PLAUSIBLE villain range bands (tight / read-stated / wide)

  This checklist applies to:
    - Calling vs cold-jams / 3-bet jams / squeezes
    - 4-bet jamming vs 3-bets
    - Reshoving over short jams
    - Iso-raising/jamming over limpers or short jams
    - Any near-all-in PFR commit

  Anti-pattern (what triggered the v7.21 fix):
    - Claude sees a hand lost large chips at PFR all-in
    - Claude labels it "punt" without doing the equity math
    - Claude invents a "detector gap" for a pattern that doesn't
      need a detector because the play is read-dependent

  Detector taxonomy guidance (v7.21):
    The cross-product of (action types: bet/call/3bet/4bet/5bet/jam/check-raise) ×
    (severity: missed/wide/tight/wrong-size) × (context: standard/squeeze/cover/micro)
    = dozens of potential detectors. DO NOT build per-spot detectors
    one-at-a-time when the pattern is read-dependent.

    Instead: rely on the existing review framework. When the analyzer
    catches an all-in spot that's outside the standard chart, the
    flag_reviewer applies the analytical checklist above. If the
    decision is dominantly -EV across plausible ranges, it stays as
    confirmed mistake. If it's read-dependent (defensible vs some
    plausible range), it gets logged to exceptions_log and removed.

    Build a new detector ONLY when:
    (a) The pattern is detectable from the hand structure alone
        (not requiring a villain-read input)
    (b) The pattern is dominantly -EV across all plausible ranges
        (i.e., it's a hard-rule violation)
    (c) The pattern occurs in 3+ sessions

    Examples of defensible new detectors:
    - "Hero opens AAo/KKo at 100BB, faces 3-bet, folds" (always wrong)
    - "Hero limp-folds at SB BvB short-handed" (always wrong)

    Examples of NON-detectors (handle via review framework, not detector):
    - "Hero 4-bet jams light at sub-30BB" (depends on villain 3-bet
      range, blockers, FE — all read-dependent)
    - "Hero calls cold-jam wide" (depends on villain range, bounty,
      coverage, blockers — all read-dependent)
    - "Hero squeezes wide MW" (depends on opener tendencies, caller
      tendencies, bounty incentives)

  Behavioral rules for Claude (documented in Quick Ref MANUAL ADD
  PROTOCOL):
    - Default classification for losing PFR all-in hands = cooler /
      variance / read-dependent, NOT punt
    - To manually-add a hand the analyzer didn't flag: FIRST ask Ron
      about villain reads, present EV across range bands (tight /
      stated read / wide), let Ron classify
    - Never claim "detector gap" without first doing the equity math
      across plausible ranges
    - Read-dependent decisions get logged to exceptions_log with
      manual_punt_overclassification tag, not flagged as punts

CHANGELOG v7.19 → v7.20:

  FLAG REVIEW LAYER (evening of 2026-04-20, Session 19 debrief):

  Architecture change: the analyzer's raw detector output is no longer
  treated as "mistakes" directly. Raw output = CANDIDATES. Every candidate
  is processed by gem_flag_reviewer.py which applies context-aware
  corrections and produces a three-tier classification:

    AUTO_CORRECTED: reviewer resolved the flag (detector bug or context
                    adjustment). NOT a real mistake — removed from leak
                    tracker.
    NEEDS_REVIEW:   reviewer couldn't fully auto-resolve; flagged for
                    Claude scrutiny using the (1) villain range,
                    (2) multi-street plan framework.
    CONFIRMED:      flag survived review. Real leak.

  Rationale: Session 19 (2026-04-19) exposed that the raw analyzer output
  produced 4 misclassifications out of 9 flagged hands — 44% false-positive
  rate. Root causes: (a) iso-raise/iso-jam conflation, (b) CVJ chart not
  context-adjusted for chip-leader cover-jams or squeeze-jams, (c) no
  bounty-cover EV adjustment, (d) double-flagging via overlapping detectors.

  New modules:
    - gem_flag_reviewer.py (450 lines): core review module implementing

    - gem_report_draft.py: renders two-tier Del 4B (Auto-Corrected →
      Needs Review → Confirmed Mistakes → Detector Bugs → Mutex Drops)

CHANGELOG v7.18 → v7.19:

  SOLVER AUGMENTATION (afternoon of 2026-04-20):
  - NEW: gem_solver.py v0.2 — exact-enumeration river solver,
    three modes: call_fold, value_bet, bluff. Uses phevaluator
    (pip dependency) for 7-card hand ranking. Computes true
    equity vs defined ranges; EV via pot-odds arithmetic.
  - NEW: gem_ranges.py — loads preflop charts from
    Poker_Ranges_Text.txt, narrows ranges street-by-street
    using hand-class keep tables (FLOP_CALL_KEEP / TURN_CALL_KEEP),
    splits river lead into value/bluff buckets. Every narrowing
    step logged to audit trail. HEURISTIC, not solver-derived.
  - NEW: gem_solver_integration.py — bridge between parsed hands
    and solver. Detects eligible river HU decisions, reconstructs
    pot/bet context from raw HH, calls solver, returns
    augmentation dict. Non-blocking: exceptions leave breadcrumb
    files, never crash the report.
  - gem_report_data.py v7.15 patch (section 10b):
      * Calls run_on_mistakes() after heuristic EV block.
      * Populates rd['solver_augmentations'] keyed by hand_id.
      * Populates rd['solver_meta'] with scan counts + scope notes.
      * Wrapped in try/except — solver failure does NOT break the
        report; heuristic EV pipeline is unaffected.
  - gem_report_draft.py patch (Del 4B):
      * New columns "Solver EV" and "Conf" on CLEAR and MARGINAL
        mistake tables.
      * Legend line above the table: "Augments heuristic EV —
        does NOT replace."
      * New section "Solver-Only River Decisions" for spots the
        solver ran on that weren't flagged as mistakes (calibration
        data — see if solver surfaces spots the heuristic misses).

  TRANSPARENCY CONTRACT (enforced for every solver run):
  Every invocation writes an audit bundle to
  /home/claude/solver_runs/<session_tag>/<hand_id>/:
    inputs.json      — spec + resolved combo counts + timestamp
    command.txt      — exact CLI call, version, timestamp
    raw_stdout.txt   — per-combo enumeration: hand_rank,
                       villain_rank, win/tie/loss — every combo
                       visible, no hidden computation
    result.json      — structured output for pipeline consumption
    caveats.txt      — 8 explicit caveats (scope, ICM, HU-only,
                       M13/M14 application, confidence tier,
                       "NOT AUTHORITATIVE FOR RULE UPDATES")
    range_audit.json — every narrowing step with input/output
                       combo counts and hand-class distribution

  SCOPE & LIMITATIONS (v7.19 — narrow by design):
  - River HU only. Flop/turn decisions not supported.
  - chipEV only. ICM-sensitive spots get solver EV, but user must
    apply ICM adjustment manually. Bubble/FT hands are flagged
    in caveats but not adjusted.
  - Ranges are HEURISTIC-CONSTRUCTED, not solver-derived. See
    gem_ranges.py narrowing tables. Review range_audit.json
    before trusting any result.
  - Hero position/sizing assumed BTN open 22% unless overridden.
    v0.3 will pull from parsed hand directly.
  - Does NOT auto-update J-rules or M-rules. Solver disagreement
    with coaching rules = discussion flag, per existing policy
    in GTO Wizard Guide §3.
  - Complements GTO Wizard, does not replace it. GTO Wizard still
    drives preflop + ICM + multiway analysis.

  KNOWN GAPS for v0.3+:
  - Villain position inferred as BB (best-guess); should be read
    from hand record once n_players_flop is tracked.
  - Open-size mapped to fixed 22% (closest BB_DEF bucket).
    Should be derived from preflop raise amount.
  - Bluff detection at range-split stage is crude (high_card or
    weak_pair bucket). Better signal: "was this a draw on turn
    that missed on river?" — requires street-by-street draw
    tracking, not implemented yet.
  - No sizing sweep. Solver evaluates only the sizing actually
    used; doesn't answer "was this the wrong SIZE?".
  - Confidence tier is based on combo count only. Should also
    factor in how many narrowing steps applied and how much
    weight was retained.

  FILES (all in /home/claude/ for prototype; ready to promote
  to /mnt/project/ once Ron reviews a few real sessions):
    gem_solver.py               (v0.2, 280 lines)
    gem_ranges.py               (v0.1, 330 lines)
    gem_solver_integration.py   (v0.1, 260 lines)
    gem_report_data.py          (patched — section 10b added)
    gem_report_draft.py         (patched — Del 4B augmented)
    test_e2e.py                 (synthesized river-call mistake)
    test_pipeline.py            (full report_data round-trip)

  DEPENDENCIES:
    pip install phevaluator --break-system-packages

    coded quartile table.

    quick-ref equity rates: preflop ahead=80%/flip=55%/behind=20%,
    postflop ahead=85%/flip=50%/behind=25%) vs actual wins for
    EAI hands. Output includes delta_wins and approx_bb_variance

For Hungry Horse rules (HH1-HH18: sizing framework, depth adjustment, underbluff catalog, bluff/value spots), see: APPENDIX L
For MechanicsOfPoker podcast rules (M1-M25: probe/delayed-cbet exploit, 3BP double-FD barrel selection, exploit-tree coherence, plan-every-street, population tendency catalog, sizing heuristics table), see: APPENDIX M
For classification rules (c-bet, river value, OAD, probes), see: CLASSIFICATION RULES
For postflop caller aggression targets (IP/OOP), see: POSTFLOP CALLER AGGRESSION TARGETS


========================================================
NEW LEARNING INTAKE CHECKLIST (v7.25 — MANDATORY PROCESS)
========================================================

PRINCIPLE: When Ron introduces a new coaching insight (Dave, Amit,
Jaka, Boivin, Hungry Horse, MoP, GTO Wizard solve, podcast, book,
live observation, or his own pattern recognition), Claude MUST walk
this 5-step checklist BEFORE writing any code or instruction changes.
Output the checklist results to Ron for confirmation, then ship.

This exists because v7.24 shipped J41-J44 as documentation only when
J43 actually warranted a detector expansion and J44 needed parser/
analyzer code. Without a structured intake, doc-only updates masquerade
as "shipped" while leaving code stale.

--------------------------------------------------------
STEP 1 — CLASSIFY THE LEARNING
--------------------------------------------------------

Source + context:
  - Source: Dave / Amit / Jaka / Boivin / HH / MoP / GTOW solve /
    podcast / book / Ron / other
  - Date received
  - Hands reviewed (list IDs if applicable)

Type (a learning can be MULTIPLE types):
  A. Principle / mental model — cannot be auto-detected
     (e.g., J42 ladder heuristic)
  B. Range / threshold update — new range definition or target
     value (e.g., J37)
  C. New auto-detectable rule — clear trigger conditions
     (e.g., J34 MP raise-or-3bet-fold)
  D. Sizing / format change — needs new parser field or sizing
     tracker (e.g., J30 BB 3-bet sizing, J44 IP 3-bet sizing)
  E. Generalization of existing rule — broadens existing detector
     trigger (e.g., J43 generalizing J34)
  F. Population / exploit insight — M-rule catalog or population
     calibration (e.g., M11 river raises value-heavy)
  G. Process / workflow change — review checklist or report
     structure (e.g., v7.21 MANUAL ADD PROTOCOL)

Conflict check:
  - Conflicts with existing rule? (Precedence: Dave > Jaka,
    ICM > chip-EV, GTOW > heuristic)
  - If conflict → state resolution explicitly in instructions

--------------------------------------------------------
STEP 2 — COMPONENT IMPACT MATRIX
--------------------------------------------------------

For each layer, mark: NONE / DOC / CODE / TEST / CONFIG

  Layer                      | File(s)                              | Typical impact
  ---------------------------|--------------------------------------|----------------
  Instructions               | GEM_Report_v7_Instructions.txt       | Appendix entry, version bump, changelog
  Quick Reference            | GEM_Quick_Reference.txt              | Summary line, target value, key rules entry
  Parser                     | gem_parser.py                        | New extracted field?
  Analyzer detectors         | gem_analyzer.py (Section 2)          | New detector or modified trigger?
  Analyzer aggregations      | gem_analyzer.py (stat builders)      | New tracker / sizing distribution?
  Report data                | gem_report_data.py                   | New derived structure for draft?
  Report draft               | gem_report_draft.py                  | New section / table / narrative line?
  Solver                     | gem_solver.py                        | EV calc affected?
  Ranges                     | Poker_Ranges_Text.txt + gem_ranges.py| Preflop range update?
  Tests                      | test_parser.py / test_detectors.py / test_metrics.py | New assertion?
  Test fixtures              | test_hands.txt / test_hands_detectors.txt | New hand needed?
  Schema                     | gem_schema.json + validate_schema.py | JSON structure change?
  Manual review checklist    | Quick Ref MANUAL ADD PROTOCOL        | New review step?
  Mental Game ref            | Mental_Game_Reference.txt            | Tilt/wellbeing pattern?
  Live ref                   | Live_Poker_Population_Reference.txt  | Live-format calibration?
  GTO Wizard guide           | GEM_GTO_Wizard_Guide.txt             | Review workflow?
  Session history schema     | session_history_*.csv                | New column?
  Target values              | Quick Ref TARGET VALUES block        | New target?

--------------------------------------------------------
STEP 3 — ASK BEFORE BUILDING
--------------------------------------------------------

For every CODE row, ASK Ron explicitly:
  - Ship now or defer? (defer → backlog with v-next tag)
  - Auto-detector or drill-only?
  - Test coverage required (the 268-assertion gate must still pass —
    test_parser.py 122, test_metrics.py 108, test_detectors.py 38)
  - Leak Validation Gate criteria (n threshold, %confirmed required
    to promote)

For every CONFIG row (target values, range thresholds), ASK:
  - Source? (Dave, GTOW solve, population data, Ron's read?)
  - Sample size / confidence? (drives whether it's a hard target
    or informational)

--------------------------------------------------------
STEP 4 — VERSION + CHANGELOG
--------------------------------------------------------

  - Version bump strategy:
    * Patch (v7.x.y): bug fix, small text change, no rule
    * Minor (v7.x): new rule(s), checklist update, doc additions
    * Major (v8): architectural change (line-based analysis,
      cross-session aggregation, etc.)
  - Write changelog entry in BOTH GEM_Quick_Reference.txt AND
    GEM_Report_v7_Instructions.txt
  - Update "Last updated" date
  - Note any pending work (e.g., "J44 detector pending parser
    extraction" → ships next cycle)

--------------------------------------------------------
STEP 5 — SHIP
--------------------------------------------------------

  - Apply changes in dependency order:
      parser → analyzer → report data → report draft → tests
  - Run full test suite if any code touched:
      python3 test_parser.py       (must pass 122/122)
      python3 test_metrics.py      (must pass 108/108)
      python3 test_detectors.py    (must pass 38/38 + new tests)
  - All tests MUST pass before files leave /home/claude/
  - Copy final files to /mnt/user-data/outputs/
  - present_files to Ron with summary
  - State pending work for next cycle

--------------------------------------------------------
CHECKLIST ANTI-PATTERNS (what NOT to do)
--------------------------------------------------------

  ❌ Skip the checklist because the rule "feels" like documentation
     only — let the matrix decide
  ❌ Apply changes without asking — Ron's read on detector vs
     drill-only matters
  ❌ Ship instructions without code when code is needed (this is
     exactly what happened with J43 in v7.24)
  ❌ Bundle a "principle" with a "detector" without separating them
     — J34/J43 are an example of the right pattern (J34 = detector,
     J43 = principle that generalizes it)
  ❌ Forget the test gate — 268-assertion suite is non-negotiable
  ❌ Defer test fixtures when shipping a detector — tests must
     ship WITH the detector, not "next cycle"

========================================================
END OF NEW LEARNING INTAKE CHECKLIST

========================================================
RULE CODE FORMAT STANDARD (v7.13 — MANDATORY)
========================================================

In EVERY output (report prose, drill questions, clinical examples,
GTO shortlist notes, console output, error flags, Quick Reference):

*** NEVER reference a coaching rule by code alone. ***
*** ALWAYS lead with plain-English description, code in parens. ***

CORRECT FORMAT:
  "Bet monotone boards IP as PFR regardless of hand (J14)"
  "Population under-bluffs rivers — fold medium hands (J19)"
  "BvB SB: limp 80% / raise 10% / fold 10% at 30-40BB (J29)"
  "3-bet at <35BB can't fold to 4-bet unless pure bluff (Amit)"

WRONG FORMAT:
  ❌ "per J14"
  ❌ "J14 applies here"
  ❌ "follow J19"
  ❌ "(J14)" as a standalone tag with no description
  ❌ "J29: limp 80%" (code first is wrong — reverse it)

RATIONALE: Reader should NEVER need to look up what a rule means.
The code is a tag for cross-reference only. The description is
what teaches. This applies to Dave rules (J1-J32), Amit rules,
Jaka rules (K1-K6), and GEM-internal rules (G-letter codes if any).

Same standard for list formats: instead of "J14: Monotone IP →
c-bet often", write "Monotone IP → c-bet often (J14)".

========================================================
LEAK VALIDATION GATE (v7.9 — NEW)
========================================================

PRINCIPLE: A stat outside target is a SIGNAL, not a confirmed
leak. Before promoting any metric to "Top 3 Leaks" or flagging
it 🔴 in the TLDR, Claude MUST inspect the underlying hands
and classify each as: confirmed mistake / borderline / correct.

If most hands pass validation, the stat is NOISE, not a leak.
Report it as: "Signal only — hand review shows X/Y correct."

VALIDATION PROTOCOL (apply to every 🔴 candidate):

  1. POSITIONAL OPEN RATES (BTN/CO/SB below target):
     - Pull all FI folds at that position.
     - Cross-check each fold against CORE and EXTENDED ranges.
     - If most folds are trash (not in any range) → NOT a leak.
       The open rate is low because card quality was low.
     - Only flag if multiple CORE range hands were folded.
     - Report: "X folds, Y in core range (CLEAR miss), Z in
       extended (marginal). Remaining W are correct folds."

  2. FOLD-TO-3BET (outside 55-65% target):
     - Pull every hand where Hero opened and faced a 3-bet.
     - Verify each hand is actually a 3-bet (not a squeeze, not
       a cold 4-bet — these are different situations).
     - For each fold: Was folding correct given hand + stack?
       QJo MP 20BB vs BB 3-bet = correct fold.
       ATs facing squeeze with cold-caller = correct fold.
       J9s facing cold 4-bet = shouldn't even count as F2-3B.
     - For each defend: Was calling/4-betting correct?
     - Report: "N opps, X folds. Y folds verified correct, Z
       questionable." With n<15, always note LOW confidence.

  3. TOP LOSING LINES (x-x-x_SD_lost, etc.):
     - Pull every hand in the line.
     - For EACH hand, evaluate:
       (a) Did Hero have equity to bet? (air on missed board = no)
       (b) Was SPR so low that betting = committing? If SPR <1
           and Hero has air, checking is correct.
       (c) Did villain also check (indicating both sides had
           showdown-value or air)? If villain checked all streets
           too, Hero may not have had a profitable bet target.
       (d) Was there a specific street where Hero should have bet?
           Only that street-action is the mistake, not the whole line.
     - Classify each hand: ✅ correct / 🟡 borderline / 🔴 miss.
     - Report: "Line has N hands. X confirmed misses, Y borderline,
       Z correct play." Only promote to Top Leak if >50% are misses.

  4. SD AGGRESSOR / CALLER IP / C-BET RATES:
     - These are aggregate rates where hand-by-hand validation is
       less critical (the rate itself tells the story).
     - BUT: if n<15, still pull the hands and verify.
     - For c-bet: check if the missed c-bets were multiway or HU,
       and whether Hero had ANY equity to c-bet with.
     - For caller IP: check if "truly passive" count excludes
       delayed c-bets correctly.

  5. SB BvB PREFLOP (J29):
     - With n<20, always LOW confidence.
     - Check stack depths — J29 (limp 80%) applies at 30-40BB.
       At <20BB, jamming > limping. At >50BB, raising wider is
       more acceptable.

REPORTING FORMAT:
  In Del 1F (Top 3 Leaks), add a "Validated?" column:
    ✅ Confirmed (>50% hands are real mistakes)
    🟡 Partial (some real, some correct — note ratio)
    ❌ Signal only (most hands validated as correct play)

  In TLDR, only flag as 🔴 if validation confirms the leak.
  If validation shows noise, flag as 🟡 with note:
    "🟡 F2-3B 27.3% (3/9) — hand review: all 3 folds correct"

EXAMPLES FROM SESSION 20260407:
  - CO Open 17.4% (Sess B): flagged 🔴 → validated → only 1
    CORE miss (JTo). Rest were trash hands. → ❌ Not a leak.
  - F2-3B 27.3%: flagged 🔴 → validated → all 3 folds correct
    (1 facing cold 4-bet). → ❌ Not a leak.
  - 3BP OOP x-x-x_SD_lost: -73.4 BB → validated → 1/3 real miss
    (AKo turn jam), 1 borderline (TT), 1 correct (Q8o air). →
    🟡 Partial (1 actionable hand, not systematic).
  - SD Aggressor 10.7%: aggregate rate, confirmed by MRV count
    (4 hands) and river audit (36% check-SDV). → ✅ Confirmed.


========================================================
CROSS-REFERENCE RULES (v6.9 — NEW)
========================================================

*** RANGE VERIFICATION (Poker_Ranges_Text.txt) ***

When evaluating ANY preflop decision (open, fold, 3-bet, jam,
defend), search Poker_Ranges_Text.txt for the relevant chart:

  1. Determine position + effective stack depth tier:
     <12BB → PUSH_10BB_{position}
     12-20BB → OPEN_10-20BB_{position}
     20-40BB → OPEN_20-40BB_{position}
     40+BB → OPEN_100BB_{position}

  2. Check if Hero's hand is in the listed range.

  3. If Hero opened a hand NOT in range → flag as wide open.
     If Hero folded a hand IN range → flag as missed open.
     If evaluating a 3-bet/flat → use FLAT3B_{depth}_{pos}vs{opener}.
     If evaluating a rejam → use REJAM_{pos}vs{opener}.
     If evaluating calling a rejam → use CALLRJ_{opener}vs{jammer}.

  4. Range file is ~90-95% accurate on play/fold. For marginal
     hands near the boundary, cross-check with coaching rules
     (Appendices A-J) and confirmed GEM rules before classifying
     as a punt. Range file is a LOOKUP, not the final verdict.

  5. When a hand IS in the range file but conflicts with a
     confirmed coaching rule (e.g., K7o shows in CO range but
     coaching says no offsuit <9 kicker), coaching rule wins.


*** MENTAL GAME INTEGRATION (Mental_Game_Reference.txt) ***

Apply mental game analysis in THREE places:

  1. DELIVERABLE 4 (Punts) — MENTAL PATTERN ANALYSIS:
     After listing the top punts, analyze the PATTERN:
     - Classify punts against the 7 tilt types (injustice,
       hate-losing, mistake, entitlement, revenge, desperation,
       running bad). Use definitions from Mental_Game_Reference.txt.
     - Check for "Regression Under Pressure" (Ron's confirmed
       pattern): escalating commitment after villain resistance.
     - Check for ALM L3 collapse: did Hero KNOW the correct play
       but fail to execute under pressure?
     - Check timing: do punts cluster late in session (fatigue/
       accumulated emotion lowering threshold)?
     - If punts follow coolers or bad beats → injustice tilt flag.
     - If punts follow Hero's own mistakes → mistake tilt flag.

  2. DELIVERABLE 7 (Action Card) — INJECTING LOGIC:
     Include 1-2 injecting logic statements based on the session's
     mental game pattern. Examples:
     - "Villain raised. Has the information changed, or am I
       reacting to resistance?"
     - "This mistake is an L3 signal, not failure."
     - "I can't control cards, only decisions."
     Personalize to the specific tilt type identified.

  3. DELIVERABLE 8 (Progress Tracker) — MENTAL TREND:
     In the trend analysis, note if punt rate is trending UP
     across consecutive sessions despite stable card quality
     (= accumulated tilt signal). Note if C-game floor is
     rising (= real improvement per inchworm model).


*** GTO HAND SELECTION (GEM_GTO_Wizard_Guide.txt) ***

At the end of the report, output a GTO REVIEW SHORTLIST:
5-10 hands selected for Ron to analyze in GTO Wizard.

SELECTION CRITERIA (priority order):
  1. RIVER DECISIONS where Hero bet/called/folded for >15BB pot.
     River errors are highest-impact and most verifiable in GTO.
  2. TURN BARREL DECISIONS: Did Hero double-barrel correctly?
     Especially equity-shift turns (flush/straight/overcard).
  3. CLOSE 3-BET/FLAT decisions where Hero's choice is debatable.
  4. Hands where Hero DEVIATED from a coaching rule — verify
     whether the rule or the deviation was correct.
  5. Any hand where Claude is <70% confident in the evaluation.

OUTPUT FORMAT:
  --- GTO REVIEW SHORTLIST ---
  1. TM### | Pos vs Pos | Hand | Board | Street + Decision | Why
  2. ...
  Priority: River first, then turn, then preflop.
  --- END SHORTLIST ---

Ron works through these in GTO Wizard between sessions and
brings results back for rule refinement.


*** GTO WIZARD EXPORT FILE (v7.9 — MANDATORY) ***

After generating the GTO Review Shortlist, ALWAYS produce a
companion .txt file containing the raw GGPoker hand histories
for all shortlisted hands. This file can be imported directly
into GTO Wizard.

FILE NAME: Claude GEM 2 GTOWizard YYYYMMDD_V{X}.txt
  YYYY = year, MM = month, DD = day of report generation
  X = version number (1, 2, 3...) if multiple files same day

GENERATION STEPS:
  1. Collect ALL hand IDs from:
     - GTO Review Shortlist (Del 7+)
     - Punts (Del 4A)
     - Mistakes — CLEAR only (Del 4B)
     - Missed River Value (Del 4B)
     - Missed Probes (Del 4B)
     - Coolers (Del 1C)
     - Any hand flagged 🔴 in Clinical Examples (Del 5)
     Deduplicate — a hand may appear in multiple lists.
  2. Search all input hand history files for those IDs.
     Split files on: re.split(r'\n\n+(?=Poker Hand #)', text)
     Match on: re.search(r'Poker Hand #(TM\d+)', block)
  3. Write matched blocks to output, separated by double newlines.
  4. Verify: count of extracted hands = count of unique IDs.
     If any are missing, report which IDs were not found.
  5. Save to /mnt/user-data/outputs/ and present to user.

The file must be EXACT raw hand history — no modifications,
no added comments, no reformatting. GTO Wizard expects the
native GGPoker format byte-for-byte.


========================================================
SELF-HEALING FRAMEWORK (v7.0 — NEW)
========================================================

The parser runs automated sanity checks after every session.
If ANY check FAILS, the report MUST address the failure before
publishing results. Do not silently output broken data.

*** PARSER SANITY CHECKS (run automatically) ***

  1. VPIP >= PFR (always). Fail = parsing error.
  2. Position distribution: each position 3-25% of hands.
  3. Open arithmetic: opens + true_missed == FI_opps per
     steal position. Fail = missed-open detection bug.
  4. WTSD 10-50% (voluntary, excl PF all-in). >50% = showdown
     detection broken. <10% = detection too strict.
  5. River semi-bluff count == 0 (always). >0 = classification
     bug (no draws on river).
  6. Premium rate 1-10%. Outside = card parsing error.
  7. Cross-session drift: flag any key metric that changed
     >20 points vs previous session.

*** REPORT-LEVEL CHECKS (Claude runs during analysis) ***

  1. Every punt candidate verified against raw preflop text.
  2. pfr field (not pf_action) used for missed-open detection.
  3. Effective stack (not Hero stack) used for all evaluations.
  4. Format tag verified on every punt.
  5. Notable hands cross-checked: if net_bb is negative but
     Hero collected chips, net_bb formula is wrong for that hand.

*** SELF-HEALING PROCESS ***

  When a check FAILS:
  1. Output the failure prominently (not buried in output).
  2. Attempt auto-fix if possible (e.g., reclassify river
     semi-bluffs as bluffs).
  3. If auto-fix not possible, flag the affected metrics as
     UNRELIABLE and explain which numbers are impacted.
  4. Log the failure in the run log for tracking.
  5. If the bug is in the parser code, note the fix needed
     so it can be patched for next session.

*** WHAT TRIGGERS A PARSER UPDATE ***

  - Any sanity check FAIL that requires a code fix.
  - New coaching rule that changes how hands are classified.
  - New metric requested for tracking.
  - Cross-session pattern where the same metric is flagged
    as UNRELIABLE in 2+ consecutive sessions.

*** SESSION WORKFLOW (v7.1) ***

  1. PARSE: Run gem_analyzer.py on uploaded hand histories.
     python3 gem_analyzer.py /path/to/hands/ session_name
     Outputs: gem_stats.json (all metrics) + gem_hands.json (hand data).

  2. GATE: Check sanity output. If any FAIL → fix before proceeding.
     Do NOT generate a report with broken data.

  3. REVIEW: Read gem_stats.json. The mistakes list is pre-classified
     (missed steals with pfr=False verified, monotone IP misses tagged).
     Fold-to-3bet details show preflop sequences for each spot.
     No separate analysis script needed — everything is in stats JSON.

  4. REPORT: Generate docx from gem_stats.json. The JSON has every
     metric organized by deliverable section. Report generator just
     formats — no recomputation.

  5. CHALLENGE: Present punts/mistakes for Ron to challenge.
     Update classifications based on feedback.

  6. CSV: Update session_history CSV with all metrics from stats JSON.


========================================================
REPORT FORMATTING RULES (v7.8 — NEW)
========================================================

*** COLOR CODING (mandatory for all tables) ***

Every metric table must use color indicators so Hero can
instantly see what's good/bad without memorizing targets:

  🟢 GREEN  = at or above target, strong performance
  🟡 YELLOW = slightly off target, monitor
  🔴 RED    = significantly off target, action needed
  ⚪ GREY   = neutral / insufficient sample

Prefer coloring the ACTUAL VALUE, not a separate status
column. E.g., show "🟢 52.1%" or "🔴 36.7%" inline in the
metric cell. This is more scannable than a separate column.
Only use a Status column when the metric itself can't carry
the color (e.g., text-only fields).

For markdown reports, use emoji or text markers:
  ✅ = green, ⚠️ = yellow, 🔴 = red, — = neutral

For docx/HTML reports, use actual background colors:
  Green: #d4edda, Yellow: #fff3cd, Red: #f8d7da, Grey: #e9ecef

Every table with a "Target" or expected range column MUST
include color coding on the values.

*** SECTION REFERENCES TO EXAMPLES ***

When a section surfaces a leak or finding that has hand
examples in Deliverable 5 (Clinical Examples), end the
section with a brief note: "→ See Clinical Examples below
for N hand replays of this leak." This helps Hero navigate
to the examples without searching.

*** PERCENTAGES OVER COUNTS ***

Always show percentages alongside counts: "0/5 (0%)" not
just "0" or "5 hands". When only counts are shown, Hero
cannot evaluate whether performance is good or bad.

*** HAND CONTEXT IN ERROR TABLES ***

Every hand flagged as a punt or mistake MUST include enough
context to review without looking up the hand:
  - Hand ID + Tournament + Date
  - Cards + Position + Stack (BB)
  - Board (if postflop)
  - Brief action summary (e.g., "opened, V 3-bet, Hero folded")
  - Verdict + Rule Tag

DO NOT use bare labels like "Missed Steal" without showing
what the hand was. Hero needs to be able to evaluate the
classification from the table alone.

*** HYPOTHESIS-DRIVEN FLAGGING ***

Before flagging any metric as a leak, ask: "What would be a
good reason for this number to be off-target?"

Examples:
  - VPIP-PFR gap high at 40BB+ → Could be correct if gap
    is explained by suited connectors + small pairs for
    set-mining. Check if the flats are profitable hands.
  - CO open rate low → Could be card-cold at CO specifically.
    Check premium frequency at that position.
  - HU c-bet low → Could be correct if many OOP spots
    (OOP checking is BY DESIGN low frequency).

Only flag as a leak if the gap cannot be explained by a
legitimate strategic reason. If uncertain, note both the
flag and the possible explanation.

*** TABLE SIZE AWARENESS (6-max / 5-max / 8-max) ***

Parser must detect table size from the hand history (number
of seats dealt). Tag each hand with table_size (5, 6, 8).

Positional targets differ by table size:
  8-max: Standard targets (as documented).
  6-max: All open ranges ~5-10% wider. BTN target ~55-60%.
    CO in 6-max ≈ HJ in 8-max (tighter).
    HJ in 6-max ≈ MP in 8-max.
  5-max: Even wider. Every position is effectively LP.

When reporting positional stats, note the table size mix.
If >30% of hands are 6-max, flag that targets need
adjustment. Do NOT compare 6-max open rates against
8-max targets without noting the difference.

*** TOP LOSING LINES IN REPORT BODY ***

The Top Losing Lines output from the parser MUST appear
in the report body (Deliverable 2 or 3). This is a core
v8 feature. Show the top 5 losing lines and top 3 winning
lines with hand count, net BB, and BB/hand.

*** CLINICAL EXAMPLES MUST INCLUDE HANDS ***

Deliverable 5 (Clinical Examples) MUST include actual hand
replays for each leak. A leak description without hands is
useless. For each of the top 3 leaks, include 3-5 specific
hand examples with:
  - Full preflop action
  - Board + street-by-street action
  - What Hero did vs what Hero should have done
  - Rule tag

If a leak has no hand examples (e.g., "missed steal" with
no specific hand to review), the parser must output the
actual hands that triggered the flag.


========================================================
DELIVERABLE 0 — TLDR (Top of Report)
========================================================

A 5-8 bullet summary. Each bullet is one clear fact.
Use line breaks between bullets. NOT a blob paragraph.

Must cover:
- Volume (hands / tournaments / bullets)
- Result direction (winning/losing)
- Card quality verdict (one line)
- Cooler count and severity (skip if normal range)
- EAI luck verdict (one line)
- The single most important leak
- The single biggest improvement
- One-sentence comparison to previous session

When mentioning a stat with a rate (e.g., coolers/100), include
whether it's above/below expected. If it's within normal range,
don't mention it — it's not noteworthy.

Example:
- 1,182 hands across 11 tournaments (17 bullets)
- Cleanest session of the project: 0 punts, 1 mistake in 1,182 hands
- Card cold: 2.6% premiums vs 4.7% expected
- 19 coolers (1.6/100 — 3x typical, heavy)
- EAI: hot in flips (65%), cold when ahead (69%)
- #1 leak: SB steal 38.9% vs 65% target
- #1 win: BTN 78.6% and CO 71.1% — first time above target
- vs S17: massive jump from 53.7%/39.6%


========================================================
DELIVERABLE 1 — EXECUTIVE SUMMARY (Tables Only)
========================================================

*** GLOBAL RULES (apply to entire report) ***

HAND REFERENCE FORMAT:
Every hand reference MUST include: Hand ID + Tournament name + Date.
Format: "TM5771407586 ($15 Mini Monday Monster Stack, Mar 31)"
Never reference a hand by ID alone.

TOURNAMENT FORMAT TAGGING:
Every tournament tagged as BOUNTY, FREEZEOUT, or SATELLITE.
This affects: squeeze/jam width, ICM pressure, punt classification.
When evaluating preflop all-ins, note format + whether Hero covers.
Flag "Format-Blind" errors where Hero played for wrong format.

A. Volume + Results Table
| Metric | Value |
Tournaments, Bullets, Hands, Buy-in range, Avg Buy-in,
Format breakdown (X Bounty / Y Freezeout / Z Satellite),
Punts/100, Mistakes/100, <12BB Violations

B. Card Quality Table
| Metric | This Session | Expected | Verdict |
Premiums (JJ+ AK): vs 4.7%.
Strong (TT 99 AQ AJs KQs): vs ~3.5%.
Premium+Strong: vs ~8.2%.
Suited: vs 23.5%. Pairs: vs 5.9%. Aces: vs 14.9%.
Trash (both <8, offsuit, unpaired). Avg rank sum: vs ~14.0.
Dry stretches (5+ consecutive trash).
Flag "CARD COLD" if premiums >20% below expected.

C. Cooler Table
| Hand ID (+ tourney + date) | Hero | Villain | Type |
Coolers/100 rate. Typical: 0.3-0.5. Above 0.6 = heavy.
Types: pair over pair, set over set, TPTK vs set/trips,
overpair vs set, straight vs flush, domination, backdoor.

D. EAI Tables (v7.2 — SPLIT BY STREET)

Two tables: Preflop and Postflop. Different classification logic.

TABLE 1 — PREFLOP ALL-INS:
| Category | Count | Won | Win% | Expected | Verdict |
Ahead (pair over pair, domination), Flipping (pair vs overcards,
race), Behind (dominated, lower pair).
Classification: higher pair/dominating Ace = "Ahead," not "Flip."
"Flipping" only makes sense preflop — this is where coin flips live.

TABLE 2 — POSTFLOP ALL-INS:
| Street | Count | Got In Good | Won | Got In Bad | Won |
"Got In Good" = Hero had the better hand at the time of the
all-in (evaluated by hand strength against the board at that
street). "Got In Bad" = Hero was behind when the money went in.
No "flipping" category — on the flop/turn/river, one player is
ahead and one is drawing or behind.

This split answers two different questions:
  - Preflop: "Am I running hot or cold on coin flips?"
  - Postflop: "When I get it in good, am I holding up?"

List all "Got In Bad" postflop hands for review — these may be
punts (getting it in with the worst hand) or unavoidable
(set over set, etc.).

E. Results Context Narrative
2-3 sentences connecting Card Quality + Coolers + EAI to explain
the session result. This is the ONLY narrative in Deliverable 1
(the TLDR handles the high-level story).

F. Top 3 Leaks Table
| Leak | Severity | BB Lost | BB/100 | Quick Fix |

G. Heuristic Cheat Sheet (3-6 bullets) — QUESTION FORMAT (v7.13)

*** MANDATORY: Frame every heuristic as a self-question, NOT a
directive. The goal is to train range-based thinking, not rote
rule-following. Directives like "bet river with TP+" are banned. ***

Format each heuristic as a 2-3 question chain Hero asks themselves
in the spot. Questions should force: (1) villain range mapping,
(2) range-wide plan, (3) sizing logic.

EXAMPLES:

  ❌ OLD (directive): "Bet river with TP+"
  ✅ NEW (question):  "What's villain's range after checking turn?
                        Which slice calls a river bet? What sizing
                        maximizes value across that range?"

  ❌ OLD: "Don't one-and-done"
  ✅ NEW: "I c-bet the flop — what's my plan if called? Which
           turn cards do I barrel vs give up? Is this a spot where
           villain folds turn to double barrels, or do they float
           too wide?"

  ❌ OLD: "C-bet monotone IP as PFR"
  ✅ NEW: "I'm IP as PFR on a monotone board — does villain x/c
           with weak flush draws enough to c-bet small, or do they
           x/r too wide? What's my turn plan if called?"

  ❌ OLD: "Fold middle pairs OOP to big bets"
  ✅ NEW: "With middle PP OOP facing this sizing — what's villain's
           value range, what's their bluff range, and is the pot
           odds vs range equity profitable? Small bet = call, big
           bet = fold typically, but why?"

Rotation rule: drop heuristics for leaks Hero has internalized
(2+ consecutive sessions with the stat in range). Add new ones
targeting the current session's top 3 leaks.

M. Board Texture Performance (v6.9)

| Board Type | Hands | C-bet% | Target CB% | Status | FaceBet Call% | bb/100 |
| Paired | | | 64-74% (sm sizing) | | | |
| Monotone | | | Check air, bet made | | | |
| Connected-Mid | | | 50% (sm sizing) | | | |
| Dry A-high | | | 70-80% (range bet) | | | |
| Dynamic (2+ broadways, 2-tone+) | | | 55-65% | | | |
| Low dry (8-high or lower) | | | 60-70% | | | |

Apply color coding to C-bet% vs Target. Show percentages not
raw counts — "7/15 (47%)" not "7". Hero needs to see whether
the percentage is within the target range at a glance.

Split columns by IP/OOP where sample ≥ 10 hands per cell.
Split rows by PFR/non-PFR where sample allows.

Board classification rules:
  Paired = any pair on board.
  Monotone = 3 cards same suit on flop.
  Connected-Mid = 3 unpaired 5-J range ≤2 gaps.
  Dry A-high = A + 2 disconnected cards (A92, A83, AK5 rainbow).
  Dynamic = 2+ broadways + flush draw possible.
  Low dry = highest card 8 or below, rainbow or 2-tone.

Cross-ref with Jaka coaching (Appendix A):
  Paired → should bet high freq, small sizing
  Monotone → check air, bet made hands
  Connected-mid → small c-bet when betting
  Dry A-high → range bet if disconnected (Dave J4)

N. River Frequency Audit (v7.0)

Track Hero's river actions when checked to AND when facing bets:

IMPORTANT: These targets are RANGES, not exact numbers that
sum to 100%. Hero can be at the lower end of every range
simultaneously and still be within acceptable bounds. Only
flag when a metric is BELOW the lower threshold or ABOVE the
upper threshold.

HERO AS BETTOR (checked to on river):
| Action | Count | % | Approx Target | Gap |
| Value bet | | | ~25-35% | |
| Bluff | | | ~10-15% | |
| Check back (SDV) | | | ~35-45% | |
| Check back (give up) | | | ~15-25% | |

NEVER classify river bets as "semi-bluff." On the river there
are no cards to come — missed draws are AIR, classified as
bluffs. Semi-bluff is a flop/turn concept only.

Key ratio: Bluff-to-Value should be ~0.4-0.6 (MDF-based).
If >0.8 → too many bluffs. If <0.2 → not bluffing enough.

HERO FACING RIVER BET:
| Action | Count | % | Approx Target | Gap |
| Fold | | | ~50-60% | |
| Call | | | ~30-40% | |
| Raise | | | ~5-10% | |

When Hero calls river and goes to showdown:
  Win% of river calls = track. Below 40% = calling too wide.
  List the 3 worst river calls (lowest hand strength at SD).

When Hero folds river:
  Pot odds implied calling frequency. If Hero folds more than
  pot odds allow, flag as over-folding.

O. Preflop Deviation Log (v7.2 — IMPLEMENTED)

Parser dynamically loads ALL ranges from Poker_Ranges_Text.txt
(117+ charts) and checks every preflop decision against the
relevant chart by position + stack depth.

SCENARIOS CHECKED:
  A. FIRST-IN: OPEN/PUSH charts by depth tier
     <12BB → PUSH_10BB_{pos}
     12-20BB → OPEN_10-20BB_{pos}
     20-40BB → OPEN_20-40BB_{pos}
     40BB+ → OPEN_100BB_{pos} (SB uses _SB_LIMP and _SB_RAISE)
     Flags: Wide Open, Missed Open

  B. FACING ONE OPEN: FLAT3B + REJAM charts
     FLAT3B_{depth_tier}_{hero_pos}vs{opener_pos}
     REJAM_{hero_pos}vs{opener_pos}
     Depth tiers: <25BB→20BB, 25-35→30BB, 35-45→40BB, 45+→50BB
     Flags: Missed Defend/3-Bet, Wide 3-Bet, Missed Rejam

  C. HERO OPENED, FACES JAM: CALLRJ charts
     CALLRJ_{hero_pos}vs{jammer_pos}
     Flags: Missed Call-Rejam, Wide Call-Rejam

  D. BB DEFENSE: BB_DEF charts by opener width
     BB_DEF_vs{opener_pct}pct (mapped from opener position)
     Flags: Missed BB Defend, Wide BB Defend

CONFIDENCE TIERS:
  CLEAR = hand is clearly in/out of range; counted as mistake.
  MARGINAL = hand is borderline (GTO mixed strategy, bottom of
    range); listed as review candidate, NOT counted as mistake.

  GTO OVERRIDE: Pocket pairs and suited hands from LP are NEVER
  flagged as CLEAR Wide Opens — GTO ranges use mixed strategies
  that fold these at some frequency, but they're profitable in
  MTT context.

  REJAM DEPTH FILTER: Only flag Missed Rejam at <35BB (CLEAR)
  or 35-50BB (MARGINAL). Above 50BB, non-all-in 3-bet or flat
  are both valid — jamming is not the only correct action.

OUTPUT: Full deviation list in stats JSON. Report summary:
| Deviation Type | Total | Clear | Marginal | Common Hands |
| Wide Open | | | | |
| Missed Open | | | | |
| Missed Defend/3-Bet | | | | |
| Wide 3-Bet | | | | |
| Missed Rejam | | | | |
| Missed Call-Rejam | | | | |
| Wide Call-Rejam | | | | |
| Missed BB Defend | | | | |
| Wide BB Defend | | | | |

REPORT DISPLAY RULES FOR DEVIATIONS:

1. SUMMARY TABLE (Deliverable 2, Section O):
   Show the deviation summary table above with color coding:
   🔴 if any CLEAR count > 0 for that type.
   🟡 if only MARGINAL deviations exist.
   ⚪ if zero deviations of that type.

2. TOP CLEAR DEVIATIONS (Deliverable 4, merged with Mistakes):
   All CLEAR deviations feed into the Mistake table (Table B).
   Include hand context: position, stack, cards, chart used,
   what Hero did vs what the range says.
   Example row:
   | TM### | 32 Bounty King | KTo | HJ | 48BB | Wide Open |
   | OPEN_100BB_HJ says fold. Hero opened, won preflop. |

3. EXAMPLE HANDS (Deliverable 5, Clinical Examples):
   For the top 2-3 deviation TYPES with the most CLEAR flags,
   include 3 hand replays each. Priority order:
   a. Wide Opens — show the hand, position, depth, what range
      says, and whether Hero profited (lucky ≠ correct)
   b. Missed Rejams — show what Hero did (flat) vs what range
      says (jam), with the opener and stack context
   c. Wide BB Defend — show what Hero called with vs the
      BB_DEF chart, and whether it cost chips
   d. Missed Defend/3-Bet — show what Hero folded that should
      have continued, with the FLAT3B chart reference

4. MARGINAL DEVIATIONS — SEPARATE SECTION:
   List MARGINAL deviations as "Review Candidates" in a
   separate table after the CLEAR mistakes. These are NOT
   counted in Mistakes/100 but Hero should scan them for
   patterns (e.g., always folding suited connectors from MP
   that the range says to open).

5. CROSS-REFERENCE WITH OTHER METRICS:
   - Wide Opens correlate with VPIP-PFR gap (opening wide
     without raising = flatting problem)
   - Missed Rejams correlate with low 3-bet rate
   - Wide BB Defend correlates with high BB VPIP
   - Missed Opens correlate with low position open rates
   Note these connections in the report narrative.

→ See Clinical Examples for hand replays of top deviations.

========================================================

Check-raise frequency tracked as CR / saw-street-hands.
Approximation (true denominator = hero-checked-and-villain-bet),
but sufficient for leak detection at session level.

TARGETS:
  Flop CR%:   6-8%  (of saw-flop hands)
  Turn CR%:   3-5%
  River CR%:  2-4%
  Total CR%:  8-12%

Below 4% flop CR = confirmed leak (no aggressive OOP line).
Above 12% flop CR = over-check-raising (investigate by position).

REPORT FORMAT: Table with Street | CRs | Saw Street | CR% | Target
with standard color coding. Auto-generated by report draft.

PREFLOP DEVIATION INTEGRATION (v7.2):
All CLEAR preflop deviations from the deviation checker are
included in Table B as mistakes. MARGINAL deviations are listed
separately as "Review Candidates" after the mistake table.
This means Wide Opens from EP/MP, Missed Rejams at <35BB, and
Missed Defend/3-Bet with hands in the REJAM range all appear
as actionable mistakes alongside postflop errors.

CRITICAL: The "Board + Action Summary" column must include enough
context for Hero to evaluate the hand without looking it up:
  - For Missed Steals: "folded K9o first-in at CO 73BB"
  - For Missed C-Bet: "Board 3h5h7h, checked IP with QJo 10BB"
  - For Missed Value: "Board Ah4dKc9s6h, TP ATo, checked river
    after 1 street of value"
  - For any postflop error: board + Hero's action + what should
    have happened

Hero must be able to agree/disagree with the classification
from the table alone without pulling up hand histories.

Must include: "If you disagree with any of these assessments 
based on table dynamics or exploitative reads I missed, reply 
with 'Challenge Rank [#]' and provide your reasoning."

Mental analysis: pattern of PUNTS (tilt?) vs MISTAKES (habit?).
Punts trigger tilt type classification.
Mistakes trigger L3→L4 mastery analysis.

MENTAL GAME PATTERN ANALYSIS (v7.0 — using Mental_Game_Reference.txt):
After the error tables, add a "Mental Pattern" section:
  1. Tilt type classification: ONLY for PUNTS. Which of the 7
     tilt types explains the punt pattern? Mistakes are NOT tilt.
  2. Timing analysis: When did PUNTS occur? Early = systemic.
     Late = fatigue/accumulated emotion. After coolers = injustice.
     (Mistakes can cluster anywhere — they're habitual, not emotional.)
  3. L3 collapse check: For each MISTAKE, did Hero KNOW the rule?
     If yes = L3→L4 mastery gap (needs reps, not coaching).
     If no = knowledge gap (needs coaching/study).
  4. Regression Under Pressure: Did any PUNT involve Hero
     escalating after villain resistance? (Ron's confirmed pattern)
  5. Accumulated tilt: Is PUNT rate trending up vs prior sessions
     with similar card quality? If yes = cup overflowing.
     (Mistake rate trending up = different signal: fatigue or
     regression to old habits.)

ERROR VERIFICATION CHECKLIST (v7.0 — MANDATORY):
Before classifying ANY hand as a punt or mistake, complete ALL steps:

  1. CHECK EFFECTIVE STACK (min of Hero and relevant villain).
  2. CHECK FORMAT (Bounty/Freezeout/Satellite).
  3. VERIFY PREFLOP ACTION from raw hand text:
     - Did Hero actually fold, or did Hero OPEN and then
       fold to a 3-bet/4-bet/jam?
     - If Hero opened (pfr=True) → NOT a "missed open."
       Evaluate as fold-to-3-bet decision instead.
     - NEVER use pf_action=='fold' alone to detect missed
       opens. Must also check pfr==False.
  4. CHECK RANGE FILE for position + depth.
  5. CROSS-CHECK with coaching rules if conflict.
  6. For postflop: verify IP/OOP, board texture, SPR.

BUG HISTORY (Session 17): 6 of 8 "punt" classifications
were false positives because the analysis used pf_action
(last action) instead of pfr (ever raised). Hero opened
all 6 hands and folded to 3-bets. Parser tracks pfr
correctly — the analysis script was wrong.


========================================================
CLASSIFICATION RULES (Session 18 Hand Review — v7.2)
========================================================
Added: 2026-04-06
Source: Ron's hand-by-hand review of Session 18 flagged hands

*** HU FLOP C-BET CLASSIFICATION ***

  STAT SPLIT: Always report HU c-bet as IP and OOP separately.
  OOP c-bet is low-frequency BY DESIGN. Do not flag OOP
  checks as mistakes. Only IP misses are actionable.

  NOT A C-BET OPPORTUNITY if villain bet first on the flop.
  Parser must check villain_bet_flop_first flag.

  WHEN CHECKING IS CORRECT (IP):
  - Middling connected board with good backdoors: check to
    keep worse hands in (AT, AJ stay in). (TM5790996947)
  - Paired board 77-JJ: DEPENDS on connectivity.
    Connected paired (886, 774, TT8): check heavy to avoid
    villain CR (villain CRs trips, straights, FDs widely).
    Disconnected paired (JJ2, QQ5, 332): range bet ~98%,
    villain CR range is narrow (trips only + some bluffs).
    (Jaka coaching + GTO confirmation)
  - Weak ace (A4, A3 type): check, not c-bet
  - Top set: check to induce (TM5793574604)
  - Condensed villain range (77 on 7h9d7c): heavy check
  - A9s on dry A-high: check to induce turn calls from
    weaker hands (TM5795179807)
  - Delayed c-bet is OK when only better hands would call
    a direct flop c-bet (TM5792661307)

  WHEN C-BET IS CORRECT (IP):
  - Monotone boards: always c-bet IP as PFR (Dave J14)
  - Low dry boards with overcards
  - A92 duotone: range bet (Dave)
  - Rainbow middling connected in satellites (TM5790998126)

  PREFLOP — BB vs BTN:
  - 22-44 with <40BB vs BTN open: SHOVE. Don't flat small
    pairs OOP at shallow depth. BTN range is wide enough
    that 22-44 has sufficient equity to jam.


*** MISSED RIVER VALUE CLASSIFICATION ***

  ONLY FLAG: Top pair+, overpair, two pair+, trips+.
  NEVER FLAG: 3rd pair or worse. "Only getting called by
  better" — Ron confirmed this is not a value bet spot.

  REPORT FORMAT: When listing missed river value hands,
  include the full action summary so Hero can review:
  | Hand ID | Cards | Pos | Strength | Streets Bet | Board | Action Summary |
  "Action Summary" = e.g., "PFR, V checked all streets,
  Hero checked back river with TPTK on safe board" or
  "Caller, Hero bet flop, checked turn/river with 2 pair."
  Hero needs to see WHY only 0-1 streets were extracted.

  DON'T FLAG 2ND PAIR WITH 2 STREETS: If Hero already
  extracted 2 streets of value with 2nd pair, that's enough.
  Two streets is the max for second pair.

  DON'T FLAG MW WEAK: Multiway pots with 2nd pair or worse
  are not missed value — too many hands beat Hero.

  CHECK DRAW COMPLETION: If the river completes a flush
  (4+ to flush on board) or straight (4 to straight), don't
  flag thin value bets. The risk outweighs the EV.


*** ONE-AND-DONE CLASSIFICATION ***

  EXCLUDE FROM OAD COUNT:
  - Check-raises: Hero CR'd flop (not a c-bet-then-check)
  - All-in on flop: no turn decision possible
  - Villain folded to flop c-bet: no turn to bet
  - Hero bet river after checking turn: delayed barrel,
    not "giving up" (Hero extracted 2 streets)

  WHEN OAD IS ACCEPTABLE:
  - Good SDV but not great (JJ on Kx board): don't barrel
    into better hands when you have showdown value
  - Monotone board where villain called flop: OK to shut
    down sometimes


*** PROBE CLASSIFICATION ***

  HU ONLY: Never flag multiway pots as missed probes.
  VILLAIN MUST HAVE CHECKED: If villain bet the flop,
  it's not a probe spot — Hero is facing a bet, not
  probing into weakness.
  HERO MUST NOT HAVE FOLDED: Can't probe if you folded.


*** FOLD-TO-3BET CLASSIFICATION ***

  EXCLUDE 4-BET FOLDS: If Hero 3-bet and then faced a
  4-bet and folded, that is fold-to-4bet, NOT fold-to-3bet.
  These are separate strategic decisions.
  Hero opening → facing 3-bet → fold = fold-to-3bet
  Hero 3-betting → facing 4-bet → fold = fold-to-4bet


*** MISSED STEAL CONFIDENCE TIERS (v7.8 — NEW) ***

  Parser splits missed steals into CLEAR and MARGINAL:
  
  CLEAR: Hand is in the CORE opening range for the position.
    These are standard opens that should almost always be
    played. Examples: K9o from CO, ATo from BTN.
    → Counted in Mistakes/100.
  
  MARGINAL: Hand is in the EXTENDED opening range (bottom
    20% of range file). These are borderline hands where
    folding may be correct with table dynamics, ICM, or
    reads. Examples: 84s from CO, T6s from CO, J8o from CO.
    → Listed separately as "review candidates," NOT counted
    in Mistakes/100.
  
  ROOT CAUSE: The range file (Poker_Ranges_Text.txt) uses
  GTO cash-game ranges at 100BB which open 46.7% from CO.
  In MTT bounty turbos, the bottom of this range is
  situational. Parser must not flag marginal range hands
  as clear mistakes.


*** TABLE SIZE AND POSITION (v7.8 — NEW) ***

  CO is CO regardless of table size. BTN is BTN. SB is SB.
  The relevant factor is players BEHIND, which is constant
  for CO/BTN/SB at any table size.

  DO NOT adjust CO/BTN/SB opening targets for 6-max or
  5-max. These positions always have the same number of
  players behind them.

  Table size DOES affect EP/MP positions (fewer players =
  fewer EP seats). Report the table size mix but do not
  use it to explain CO/BTN/SB open rates.


*** DELAYED C-BET EXCLUSION (v7.8 — NEW) ***

  When calculating Caller IP Flop Aggression, EXCLUDE
  hands where Hero checked the flop but bet the turn
  (delayed c-bet). These are not passive — Hero chose to
  delay aggression to a better street.

  Report format: "0/13 (0%) — 3 delayed cbets, 10 truly
  passive" to distinguish active delay from passivity.


*** MISSED RIVER VALUE — KICKER QUALITY (v7.8 — NEW) ***

  Only flag river check-backs as missed value if Hero has:
  - Trips or better: always flag
  - Two pair: only if BOTH hole cards pair the board (real
    two-pair, not board-driven)
  - Top pair: only with GOOD kicker (T or higher = TPGK+)
  - Overpair: always flag
  
  DO NOT flag:
  - TPOK (ok kicker, 7-9): "what worse calls?" too thin
  - TPWK (weak kicker, 2-6): way too thin
  - Board-driven two-pair where only one hole card pairs
  - 3rd pair or worse (existing rule)
  - ANY hand on board with 4+ broadways (too many better
    hands possible)
  
  ROOT CAUSE: Previously flagged all TP+ as missed value.
  But TPOK on a broadway-heavy board (A4s on 2c8hJsQsAd)
  has almost nothing that calls worse. Kicker quality
  determines whether a river bet is value or turning your
  hand into a bluff.


*** POSTFLOP CALLER AGGRESSION TARGETS (Session 18 — v7.3) ***

  KEY FINDING: Hero's caller flop aggression IP is 14% (target
  30-40%). Draws are bet at 0% IP. This is the largest
  controllable EV leak in the session.

  IP/OOP DISTINCTION (critical):
  - IP draws: semi-bluff. You have fold equity + draw equity +
    position. Betting is correct at GTO frequencies.
  - OOP draws: check-call for equity realization (Dave J17).
    Don't bet/raise and risk getting raised off your draw.
    Exception: combo draws (FD+OESD) can lead/CR OOP.

  IP CALLER TARGETS (by draw type on flop):
    Made hand (pair+)     50-55%   ← biggest gap (was 26%)
    Nut flush draw         65-70%
    Flush draw             55-60%
    OESD + BDFD           60-65%
    OESD                   60-65%
    Gutshot + BDFD        45-50%
    Gutshot               35-40%
    BDFD only             30-35%
    Overcards             30-35%

  REPORT FORMAT: Show as "X/Y (Z%)" with color coding:
    🟢 = within 10pts of target
    🟡 = 10-20pts below target
    🔴 = 20+ pts below target or 0%
  Example: "Made hand: 0/5 (0%) 🔴 [target 50-55%]"

  OOP CALLER TARGETS:
    Made hand (pair+)     10-15%   (check-raise line, not lead)
    All draws             Check-call (Dave J17)
    Exception             Combo draws (FD+OESD) can CR

  IP CALLER TARGETS (turn):
    Made hand              50%
    Nut FD / FD           55-65%
    OESD                   55-60%
    Gutshot               30-35%
    Overcards             15-20%

  POPULATION EXPLOIT: Villains at $10-$88 under-bluff (J19),
  which means they OVER-FOLD. Hero's bluffs are MORE profitable
  than GTO. Target: GTO or +5-10% above on flop when IP.
  When FACING villain aggression: tighten up (J19).

  TRACKED METRIC: Caller_IP_Flop_Agg in session_history CSV.
  Parser outputs aggression_tables in gem_stats.json with
  full draw-type breakdown by Role/Street/Position.
